239   private static int [] zzUnpackAction() {
240     int [] result = new int[1750];
241     int offset = 0;
242     offset = zzUnpackAction(ZZ_ACTION_PACKED_0, offset, result);
243     return result;
244   }
245 
246   private static int zzUnpackAction(String packed, int offset, int [] result) {
247     int i = 0;       /* index in packed string  */
248     int j = offset;  /* index in unpacked array */
249     int l = packed.length();
250     while (i < l) {
251       int count = packed.charAt(i++);
252       int value = packed.charAt(i++);
253       do result[j++] = value; while (--count > 0);
254     }
255     return j;
256   }

485   private static int [] zzUnpackRowMap() {
486     int [] result = new int[1750];
487     int offset = 0;
488     offset = zzUnpackRowMap(ZZ_ROWMAP_PACKED_0, offset, result);
489     return result;
490   }
491 
492   private static int zzUnpackRowMap(String packed, int offset, int [] result) {
493     int i = 0;  /* index in packed string  */
494     int j = offset;  /* index in unpacked array */
495     int l = packed.length();
496     while (i < l) {
497       int high = packed.charAt(i++) << 16;
498       result[j++] = high | packed.charAt(i++);
499     }
500     return j;
501   }

3870   private static int [] zzUnpackTrans() {
3871     int [] result = new int[341204];
3872     int offset = 0;
3873     offset = zzUnpackTrans(ZZ_TRANS_PACKED_0, offset, result);
3874     offset = zzUnpackTrans(ZZ_TRANS_PACKED_1, offset, result);
3875     return result;
3876   }
3877 
3878   private static int zzUnpackTrans(String packed, int offset, int [] result) {
3879     int i = 0;       /* index in packed string  */
3880     int j = offset;  /* index in unpacked array */
3881     int l = packed.length();
3882     while (i < l) {
3883       int count = packed.charAt(i++);
3884       int value = packed.charAt(i++);
3885       value--;
3886       do result[j++] = value; while (--count > 0);
3887     }
3888     return j;
3889   }

3927   private static int [] zzUnpackAttribute() {
3928     int [] result = new int[1750];
3929     int offset = 0;
3930     offset = zzUnpackAttribute(ZZ_ATTRIBUTE_PACKED_0, offset, result);
3931     return result;
3932   }
3933 
3934   private static int zzUnpackAttribute(String packed, int offset, int [] result) {
3935     int i = 0;       /* index in packed string  */
3936     int j = offset;  /* index in unpacked array */
3937     int l = packed.length();
3938     while (i < l) {
3939       int count = packed.charAt(i++);
3940       int value = packed.charAt(i++);
3941       do result[j++] = value; while (--count > 0);
3942     }
3943     return j;
3944   }

4003    * Chars in class \p{Line_Break = Complex_Context} are from South East Asian
4004    * scripts (Thai, Lao, Myanmar, Khmer, etc.).  Sequences of these are kept 
4005    * together as as a single token rather than broken up, because the logic
4006    * required to break them at word boundaries is too complex for UAX#29.
4007    * <p>

4051   /** 
4052    * Unpacks the compressed character translation table.
4053    *
4054    * @param packed   the packed character translation table
4055    * @return         the unpacked character translation table
4056    */
4057   private static char [] zzUnpackCMap(String packed) {
4058     char [] map = new char[0x10000];
4059     int i = 0;  /* index in packed string  */
4060     int j = 0;  /* index in unpacked array */
4061     while (i < 3010) {
4062       int  count = packed.charAt(i++);
4063       char value = packed.charAt(i++);
4064       do map[j++] = value; while (--count > 0);
4065     }
4066     return map;
4067   }
4068 
4069 
4070   /**
4071    * Refills the input buffer.
4072    *
4073    * @return      <code>false</code>, iff there was new input.
4074    * 
4075    * @exception   java.io.IOException  if any I/O-Error occurs
4076    */
4077   private boolean zzRefill() throws java.io.IOException {
4078 
4079     /* first: make room (if you can) */
4080     if (zzStartRead > 0) {
4081       System.arraycopy(zzBuffer, zzStartRead,
4082                        zzBuffer, 0,
4083                        zzEndRead-zzStartRead);
4084 
4085       /* translate stored positions */
4086       zzEndRead-= zzStartRead;
4087       zzCurrentPos-= zzStartRead;
4088       zzMarkedPos-= zzStartRead;
4089       zzStartRead = 0;
4090     }
4091 
4092     /* is the buffer big enough? */
4093     if (zzCurrentPos >= zzBuffer.length) {
4094       /* if not: blow it up */
4095       char newBuffer[] = new char[zzCurrentPos*2];
4096       System.arraycopy(zzBuffer, 0, newBuffer, 0, zzBuffer.length);
4097       zzBuffer = newBuffer;
4098     }
4099 
4100     /* finally: fill the buffer with new input */
4101     int numRead = zzReader.read(zzBuffer, zzEndRead,
4102                                             zzBuffer.length-zzEndRead);
4103 
4104     if (numRead > 0) {
4105       zzEndRead+= numRead;
4106       return false;
4107     }
4108     // unlikely but not impossible: read 0 characters, but not at end of stream    
4109     if (numRead == 0) {
4110       int c = zzReader.read();
4111       if (c == -1) {
4112         return true;
4113       } else {
4114         zzBuffer[zzEndRead++] = (char) c;
4115         return false;
4116       }     
4117     }
4118 
4119     // numRead < 0
4120     return true;
4121   }
4122 
4123     
4124   /**
4125    * Closes the input stream.
4126    */
4127   public final void yyclose() throws java.io.IOException {
4128     zzAtEOF = true;            /* indicate end of file */
4129     zzEndRead = zzStartRead;  /* invalidate buffer    */
4130 
4131     if (zzReader != null)
4132       zzReader.close();
4133   }
4134 
4135 
4136   /**
4137    * Resets the scanner to read from a new input stream.
4138    * Does not close the old reader.
4139    *
4140    * All internal variables are reset, the old input stream 
4141    * <b>cannot</b> be reused (internal buffer is discarded and lost).
4142    * Lexical state is set to <tt>ZZ_INITIAL</tt>.
4143    *
4144    * Internal scan buffer is resized down to its initial length, if it has grown.
4145    *
4146    * @param reader   the new input stream 
4147    */
4148   public final void yyreset(java.io.Reader reader) {
4149     zzReader = reader;
4150     zzAtBOL  = true;
4151     zzAtEOF  = false;
4152     zzEOFDone = false;
4153     zzEndRead = zzStartRead = 0;
4154     zzCurrentPos = zzMarkedPos = 0;
4155     yyline = yychar = yycolumn = 0;
4156     zzLexicalState = YYINITIAL;
4157     if (zzBuffer.length > ZZ_BUFFERSIZE)
4158       zzBuffer = new char[ZZ_BUFFERSIZE];
4159   }
4160

4190    * matched text. 
4191    * 
4192    * It is equivalent to yytext().charAt(pos), but faster
4193    *
4194    * @param pos the position of the character to fetch. 
4195    *            A value from 0 to yylength()-1.
4196    *
4197    * @return the character at position pos

4199   public final char yycharat(int pos) {

4206    */

4208     return zzMarkedPos-zzStartRead;
4209   }
4210 
4211 
4212   /**
4213    * Reports an error that occured while scanning.
4214    *
4215    * In a wellformed scanner (no or only correct usage of 
4216    * yypushback(int) and a match-all fallback rule) this method 
4217    * will only be called with things that "Can't Possibly Happen".
4218    * If this method is called, something is seriously wrong
4219    * (e.g. a JFlex bug producing a faulty scanner etc.).
4220    *
4221    * Usual syntax/scanner level error handling should be done
4222    * in error fallback rules.
4223    *
4224    * @param   errorCode  the code of the errormessage to display
4225    */
4226   private void zzScanError(int errorCode) {
4227     String message;
4228     try {
4229       message = ZZ_ERROR_MSG[errorCode];
4230     }
4231     catch (ArrayIndexOutOfBoundsException e) {
4232       message = ZZ_ERROR_MSG[ZZ_UNKNOWN_ERROR];
4233     }
4234 
4235     throw new Error(message);
4236   } 
4237 
4238 
4239   /**
4240    * Pushes the specified amount of characters back into the input stream.
4241    *
4242    * They will be read again by then next call of the scanning method
4243    *
4244    * @param number  the number of characters to be read again.
4245    *                This number must not be greater than yylength()!
4246    */
4247   public void yypushback(int number)  {
4248     if ( number > yylength() )
4249       zzScanError(ZZ_PUSHBACK_2BIG);
4250 
4251     zzMarkedPos -= number;
4252   }
4253 
4254 
4255   /**
4256    * Resumes scanning until the next regular expression is matched,
4257    * the end of input is encountered or an I/O-Error occurs.
4258    *
4259    * @return      the next token
4260    * @exception   java.io.IOException  if any I/O-Error occurs
4261    */
4262   public int getNextToken() throws java.io.IOException {
4263     int zzInput;
4264     int zzAction;
4265 
4266     // cached fields:
4267     int zzCurrentPosL;
4268     int zzMarkedPosL;
4269     int zzEndReadL = zzEndRead;
4270     char [] zzBufferL = zzBuffer;
4271     char [] zzCMapL = ZZ_CMAP;
4272 
4273     int [] zzTransL = ZZ_TRANS;
4274     int [] zzRowMapL = ZZ_ROWMAP;
4275     int [] zzAttrL = ZZ_ATTRIBUTE;
4276 
4277     while (true) {
4278       zzMarkedPosL = zzMarkedPos;
4279 
4280       yychar+= zzMarkedPosL-zzStartRead;
4281 
4282       zzAction = -1;
4283 
4284       zzCurrentPosL = zzCurrentPos = zzStartRead = zzMarkedPosL;
4285   
4286       zzState = ZZ_LEXSTATE[zzLexicalState];
4287 
4288       // set up zzAction for empty match case:
4289       int zzAttributes = zzAttrL[zzState];
4290       if ( (zzAttributes & 1) == 1 ) {
4291         zzAction = zzState;
4292       }
4293 
4294 
4295       zzForAction: {
4296         while (true) {
4297     
4298           if (zzCurrentPosL < zzEndReadL)
4299             zzInput = zzBufferL[zzCurrentPosL++];
4300           else if (zzAtEOF) {
4301             zzInput = YYEOF;
4302             break zzForAction;
4303           }
4304           else {
4305             // store back cached positions
4306             zzCurrentPos  = zzCurrentPosL;
4307             zzMarkedPos   = zzMarkedPosL;
4308             boolean eof = zzRefill();
4309             // get translated positions and possibly new buffer
4310             zzCurrentPosL  = zzCurrentPos;
4311             zzMarkedPosL   = zzMarkedPos;
4312             zzBufferL      = zzBuffer;
4313             zzEndReadL     = zzEndRead;
4314             if (eof) {
4315               zzInput = YYEOF;
4316               break zzForAction;
4317             }
4318             else {
4319               zzInput = zzBufferL[zzCurrentPosL++];
4320             }
4321           }
4322           int zzNext = zzTransL[ zzRowMapL[zzState] + zzCMapL[zzInput] ];
4323           if (zzNext == -1) break zzForAction;
4324           zzState = zzNext;
4325 
4326           zzAttributes = zzAttrL[zzState];
4327           if ( (zzAttributes & 1) == 1 ) {
4328             zzAction = zzState;
4329             zzMarkedPosL = zzCurrentPosL;
4330             if ( (zzAttributes & 8) == 8 ) break zzForAction;
4331           }
4332 
4333         }
4334       }
4335 
4336       // store back cached position
4337       zzMarkedPos = zzMarkedPosL;
4338 
4339       switch (zzAction < 0 ? zzAction : ZZ_ACTION[zzAction]) {
4340         case 1: 
4341           { /* Break so we don't hit fall-through warning: */ break;/* Not numeric, word, ideographic, hiragana, or SE Asian -- ignore it. */
4342           }
4343         case 12: break;
4344         case 2: 
4345           { return WORD_TYPE;
4346           }
4347         case 13: break;
4348         case 3: 
4349           { return NUMERIC_TYPE;
4350           }
4351         case 14: break;
4352         case 4: 
4353           { return KATAKANA_TYPE;
4354           }
4355         case 15: break;
4356         case 5: 
4357           { return SOUTH_EAST_ASIAN_TYPE;
4358           }
4359         case 16: break;
4360         case 6: 
4361           { return IDEOGRAPHIC_TYPE;
4362           }
4363         case 17: break;
4364         case 7: 
4365           { return HIRAGANA_TYPE;
4366           }
4367         case 18: break;
4368         case 8: 
4369           { return HANGUL_TYPE;
4370           }
4371         case 19: break;
4372         case 9: 
4373           { return EMAIL_TYPE;
4374           }
4375         case 20: break;
4376         case 10: 
4377           { return URL_TYPE;
4378           }
4379         case 21: break;
4380         case 11: 
4381           // lookahead expression with fixed base length
4382           zzMarkedPos = zzStartRead + 6;
4383           { return WORD_TYPE;
4384           }
4385         case 22: break;
4386         default: 
4387           if (zzInput == YYEOF && zzStartRead == zzCurrentPos) {
4388             zzAtEOF = true;
4389               {
4390                 return YYEOF;
4391               }
4392           } 
4393           else {
4394             zzScanError(ZZ_NO_MATCH);
4395           }
4396       }
4397     }
4398   }
4399 
4400 
4401 }
